is one of the most played board games in the world, play with your friends, try to defeat your opponents with strategy, reasoning and a little bit of luck.\r\nGeneral rules of dominoes:\r\n- Blocking game\r\nThe most basic dominos variant is for two players and requires a double six set. The 28 domino tiles are shuffled face down and form the stock or boneyard. Each player draws seven tiles; the remainder are not used. Once the players begin drawing tiles, they are typically placed on-edge before the players, so that each player can see his own domino tiles, but none can see the value of other players' tiles. Every player can thus see how many tiles remain in the other players' hands at all times during gameplay. One player begins by downing (playing the first tile) one of their tiles. In different games first tiles are also different. In Muggins player should start with the highest double (6-6), in Bergen the first move should be 0-0, in Mexican train each round starts with the next lower double. This tile starts the line of play, a series of tiles in which adjacent tiles touch with matching, i.e. equal, values. The players alternately extend the line of play with one tile at one of its two ends. The game ends when one player wins by playing their last tile, or when the game is blocked because neither player can play. If that occurs, whoever caused the block gets all of the remaining player points not counting their own.\r\n- Scoring game\r\nPlayers accrue points during game play for certain configurations, moves, or emptying one's hand. Most scoring games use variations of the draw game. In Muggins (All fives) player must make the open ends of the layout add up to 5s or a multiple of five (5s, 10, 15, 20, etc.) In bergen player scores when numbers on the open ends are equal. If a player does not call \"domino\" before the tile is laid on the table, and another player says 'domino' after the tile is laid, the first player must pick up an extra domino. In Mexican train the double zero domino is scored as 50 points.\r\n- Draw game\r\nIn a draw game (blocking or scoring), players are additionally allowed to draw as many tiles as desired from the stock before playing a tile. The score of a game is the number of pips in the losing player's hand plus the number of pips in the stock. Most rules prescribe that two tiles need to remain in the stock. The Draw game is often referred to as simply \"dominos\".\r\n\r\nIf you like board games like Checkers, Mahjong, Backgammon and Chess, you will love Dominoes: Best Classic Dominoes Board Game.","ProductFamilyName":"Games","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ProductId":"9MT92N26MHFR","TileLayout":"Poster","Title":"Golf Battle 3D","Images":[{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.5307.13816880243720198.8f2ef58f-d174-4da1-9896-2d1fd38f09fe.fac5a049-8540-4df0-9597-4d158b032e33","Height":300,"Width":300,"BackgroundColor":"#FFFFFF","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.26914.13816880243720198.8f2ef58f-d174-4da1-9896-2d1fd38f09fe.d95ca052-2326-48d8-9849-a96506bbf23a","Height":300,"Width":620,"BackgroundColor":"#FFFFFF","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""}],"DisplayPrice":"Тегін","Price":0.0,"AverageRating":0.0,"RatingsCount":"0","PackageFamilyNames":["44511HappyDragonInc.GolfBattle3D_ffz6r8qf25722"],"ContentIds":["31a5fb02-31ab-2387-3549-9a221dc60e85","71a746dd-1690-1dfa-2502-2a75c8579985"],"GamingOptionsXboxLive":false,"AvailableDevicesDisplayText":"","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"Компьютер","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"Golf Battled 3D - Join the most exciting Golf ever! It's on the shallow end of complexity. \r\n\r\nThe objective of the game is to get rid of your cards fast to win this game! \r\n\r\nBut Uno Classic game not just a feast of fun – it also helps develop kids counting, matching, critical thinking, and social interaction.\r\n\r\nUno is a simple color and number matching game. The deck consists of 108 cards, of which there are 25 of each color (red, green, blue, and yellow), each color having two of each rank except zero. The ranks in each color are zero to nine, \"Skip\", \"Draw Two\", and \"Reverse\" (the last three being \"action cards\"). In addition, the deck contains four each of \"Wild\" and \"Wild Draw Four\" cards\r\n\r\nEach player is dealt 7 cards and the remaining cards are placed face down to form a draw pile. \r\nThe first player has to match the card in the discard pile either by number or color or the player can throw down a Wild Card else he must pick a card from the draw pile. If he can play what is drawn, great. Otherwise play moves to the next person.\r\n\r\nIn Uno The card deck contains four colors with numbers from 0 to 9, as well as Action cards - \"Reverse\", \"Skip\", \"Take Two\", \"Wild\" and \"Wild Take Four\".\r\n\r\nThe winner is first one who has no cards left. \r\n\r\nNow you can play Uno Classic with your Facebook friends, against the computer or with millions of Uno players around the world.\r\n\r\nYou can also create a Private Room and invite your friends to play.\r\n\r\nThe biggest advantage of Uno Classic card game is that it can be enjoyed by everybody in the family. Ол PLATO жүйелерінде 512 * 512 монохромды дисплейде ойын карточкаларын оңай танылатын графикалық кескіндерді көрсету алды 1978 Alfille Платон білім беру компьютерлік жүйесі үшін TUTOR бағдарламалау тілінде оған бiрiншi компьютерлік болжамдарын жүзеге асырды.\r\n\r\nБұл бастапқы FreeCell қоршаған ортаны стандартты 8 * 4 ойында қосымша 4C10 бағандар мен 1C10 жасушаларының ойындар мүмкіндік берді.
